The following actions are running on Node.js 20 and may not work as expected: actions/checkout@v4, actions/setup-go@v5, actions/setup-node@v4, actions/setup-python@v5. Actions will be forced to run with Node.js 24 by default starting June 2nd, 2026. Node.js 20 will be removed from the runner on September 16th, 2026. Once Node.js 24 becomes the default, you can temporarily opt out by setting ACTIONS_ALLOW_USE_UNSECURE_NODE_VERSION=true.
